Forks: 1

License: MIT License

MicroGO is a web application framework written in Go (Golang). I took some of the most valuable features in Laravel and implemented similar functionality in Go. Since Go is compiled and type-safe, web applications written in this language are typically much faster and far less error-prone than an equivalent application, like Laravel, written in PHP.

<a name="repo-fsfvnaulldkj5dgk6k2xfhgx"></a>
## heiyeluren/xmm

Repository: [heiyeluren/xmm](https://github.com/heiyeluren/xmm)

Author: [heiyeluren](https://github.com/heiyeluren)

Stars: 797

Forks: 87

License: Apache License 2.0

XMM is a high performance third party memory manager for Go environments that is not affected by Gc and guarantees high performance.  XMM是一个在Go语言环境中完全自主实现的第三方内存管理库，不依赖于Go本身的任何内存管理能力，纯自主实现能够应对各种场景下大小内存的 分配/释放 工作，能自主构建高性能的 链表/树/哈希表等各类数据结构，能良好完美的逃逸掉Go内置的GC机制，是构建高性能程序基础设施。

[✅ Return to Go](#go)

## AcrylicShrimp/clr-parser-generator

Forks: 0
